 swayamsevi sanghathan maas for awarenes dwaara sanchalit research centre ‘centre for demokrasi and pis’ dwaara 15veen loksabhaa ke puure paanch saal ke kaam-kaaj par taiyaar report 'ripregentative at work' se pataa chalata he ki sansad ke tamaam diggaj janata ke prati apane dayitvon ko lekar laaparvaah hai
 There are 55 mps including Congress President Smt
 Sonia Gandhi, party vice-president Rahul Gandhi, Samajwadi Party chief Mulayam Singh who have not asked a single question in five years
 is report ko guuruuvaar ko loksabhaa kii spikar sumitra mahajan ne jari kiya
 In this report, the five-year tenure of Lok Sabha mps has been tested on various democratic parameters like their participation in debate, presence in the House, spending of MP Development Fund, disruption of proceedings, exit and private member bill
 loksabhaa main puche gaye prashnon ke lihaaj se dekhen to shivasena ke aanandarav adsul 1,280 prashn puch kar pehle number par rahe
 The report's data says that mps from Lakshadweep, Maharashtra, Kerala, Odisha, Gujarat, and Tamil Nadu asked the most questions
 prashnkaal ke kai dilachasp pahalu bhi hai jaise ki vyavsaay ke mutabik dekhen to audyogic prishthbhumi se jude saansadon ne ausatan 447 sawaal puche or loksabhaa main sabase zyada sawaal vitt vishay par hi puche gaye
 Most questions were also raised on Railways, HR, Home Ministry, Health and Agriculture, while mps saw very less interest in Parliamentary Affairs, Space, Prime Minister's Office and North East regions
 sansad main bahes ke maamalon main adhiktar loksabhaa saansadon kii bhagidaari acchhee rahi he

 Our mps have been able to spend 30% of the total MP Development Fund in five years
 tabhi to 15veen loksabhaa ke sthagan ke baad 1 march 2014 tak ke aankadon ke hisaab se abantit 19 karod rupee main se sonia gandhi ne maatr 69 pratishat, rahul gandhi ne 61 pratishat, adwani ne 57 pratishat, mulaayam singh yadav ne 76 pratishat, sharad yadav ne 62 pratishat, sharad pavaar ne 67 pratishat raashi hi kharch kii hai, vahiin duusari taraf trinmul krongress ke govindchandra, diemke ke abdul rahamaan, congress ke premuchandra guddu, trinmul congress kii dow kakoli ghosh, congress ke ajay maakan va bijepi kii sushamaa swaraj ne saansad vikaas nidhi kharch karne main kramshah baaji maari
 Senior and veteran leaders are seen serious in terms of attendance in Parliament like Sumitra Mahajan 87 percent, Mulayam Singh Yadav 85 percent, Murli Manohar Joshi 84 percent, Sharad Yadav were present in the House for 83 percent of the time but during this period Sonia Gandhi and Rahul Gandhi Attendance was less than 50 percent
 duusari taraf congress ke capi dhanapalan ekmaatr aise saansad hai jinaki upasthiti 100 fisadi darj hui
 In terms of age, the attendance of mps from 25 to 40 years was 67 percent while the attendance of mps from 41 to 60 years and above 60 years was 72 and 74 percent respectively
 vyavsaay ke anusaar saansadon kaa vishleshan kiya jaae to filmi prishthbhumi se jude saansad 57 fisadi upasthiti ke saath sabase phiseddi rahe

 report ke aankade bhi isi baat kii gavaahi dete hai
 The Lok Sabha was interrupted 51,593 times in five years, while the proceedings had to be postponed 570 times

 twitor par kai logon ne thank you piem kaa hashtag bhi chalaaya or piem modi ne bhi kaha ki shukriya sena or hamaari seva bhav kii parampara kaa
 After India's initiative, now all the countries of the world and agencies of the United Nations have also become active to help Nepal
 china ne bhi 62 sadasyon kii ek search team bheji he
 China has also sent emergency tents, generators and blanket clothes
 china ne 30 lakh dollar kii madad raashi dene kii ghoshnaa kii he
 Israel has also sent a team of 260 members consisting of 122 doctors, nurses and paramedics
 iske alaava pakistan, britain, bhutan, japan, singapore malaysia kai chote bade desh nepal kii madad ke liye aage aae hai
 According to UN agencies, the situation is so bad that rural areas of Nepal, including Kathmandu, will have to provide food and medicine for months
 bharat main bhi 72 logon kii bukamp se maut hui he
 Sitamarhi, East Champaran and Darbhanga in Bihar have suffered more
 pashchim bengal ke siliguri main bhi kai log ghayal hue hai
 The Parliament of India has expressed its condolences to the bereavement of Nepal and mps of all parties have decided to pay their one month's salary for rehabilitation work in Nepal and India
 jin saansadon ko ham din raat ulaahna dete rahe hai wo bhi aage aae hai
 Everyone accepted this proposal of Vekaiah Naidu in an instant
 bukamp kab aayega ye koi nahin bataa saktaa lekin himalay ke ilaake main bukamp aayega yah sabko pataa he
 According to scientists, about 500 million years ago, the Earth was divided into two large continents
 
 
 uresia or gondvanaa land
 In the course of development of the earth, Gondwana land broke into many pieces and moved towards different directions
 iskaa ek hissaa jo bhartiya upmahadweep bana wo urasian plate se takaraayaa
 The folds formed by the same bump and rub between the two plates form the Himalayas
 bhartiya plate aaj bhi paanch centimetre prati varsh kii dar se urasian plate par dabaav bana rahi he, yaa kahen ki uske neeche khisak rahi he
 Earthquakes occur here when the energy released between the two plates is released while staying under the hidden energy
 is himalayan ilaake main aath kii tivrata ke aasapaas ke bukamp aate rahe hai
 Such as Kangra in 1905, bihar-nepal border in 1934, Shillong in 1897 and Assam in 1950
 lekin is graphix main jo aap laal lakeer dekh rahe hai vahaan aath kii tivrata kaa bukamp beete qareeb do sau saal main nahin aayaa he
 a recent earthquake has occurred at the eastern end of this line
 bhuvaigyanikon ke mutabik is laal lakeer jise central sizmik gap kehete hai us par bada bukamp aane kii ashanka lagaataar bani hui he kyonki yahaan zamin ke neeche kaafii dabaav bana hua he or isaki urja kabhi bhi kisi bukamp kii shakl le sakati he
 a large part of India is covered by this red streak, ie the Central Scientific Gap
 himalay kaa ilaaka to sakriy zone he lekin gondvanaa to saath karod saal purana he, jo duniya kaa sabase sthir or sthaayee bhukhand he vahaan bhi bhuncup aa gaya
 The earthquakes in Koyna and Latur in Maharashtra shocked everyone
 philhal himalay or uresia plate kii dhakka mukki main ham sabaki jaan ataki hui he
 The house of our dreams hangs
 har bukamp ke baad ham sab apane hi ghar main beghar mahasoos karne lagate hai
 The roof of the house which we feel safe is deadly these days
 aap pichley do teen dinon se akhabaaron main pard rahe hai ki purvi se uttar bharat ke bade hisse ko sismik zone chaar or paanch main baanta gaya he
 The area where your anchor lives and another panelist of today does not know who trusts
 pichley do dinon se jis kisi ko dekh rahaa hum wo apane flats ko shaq kii nazar se dekh rahaa he
 Experts say that if an earthquake strikes, it should be seated at the corner of walls inside the house
 sar jhukaa liya jaae or mumkin ho to kisi chiz se dhank liya jaae
 It is also advisable to sit under the table, but when you looked at your table, it felt that it could barely handle the crockery, it would be further subdued by concrete
 lihaaza kone or teble ko chhod aapkaa yah ankar lift kii taraf bhaaga, jab khyaal aayaa ki lift khatarnaak he to sidhiyon se utarane laga
 Repeated this mistake twice
 baahar nikal kar dekha to main akelaa nahin tha
 Like me, most people did the same thing
 tippaniyan If this is an earthquake affected area then we need to be educated again and again
 sirf oonchi imaaraton kii baat nahin he, gali mohalle or dukaanon kii imaaraten bhi surakshit hai yaa nahin, kisi guideline ke aadhaar par banati hai yaa nahin yah sab lagaataar jaanane or dekhne kii zarurat he
 Twenty percent of the world's earthquakes occur in Japan
 yahaan bukamp kii tivrata 6 yaa usase zyada hoti he
 In total, there are more than 2000 tremors every year
 2011 ke bukamp or tsunami main vahaan 18000 logon kii maut ho gai thi
 Fewer people died due to the earthquake
 tsunami se zyada
 Japan buildings are considered the best in terms of anti-earthquake technology
 japani imaaraton kii neenv kaaphi gahari hoti he, shock abzarwar lage hote hai
 Buildings move along the earth so they avoid falling
 har skool ke bachche ko pataa hota he ki dharti hilne par kya karnaa he
 There is a drill in the school every month
 japan ne 1995 ke bukamp ke baad kaaphi kuch niyam banaae or apana tarika badla he
 As a civil society, how Indians behave differently from Japanese
 japani system kya he
 This is also talked about in prime time
 nepal main bukamp se marane waalon kii sankhya badhkar 3700 se zyada ho gai he
 So far more than 6500 injured have been detected
 2500 bharatiyon ko vahaan se nikaala ja chukaa he
 India has sent a team of 285 members including doctors and paramedics
 andiaref ne kaha he ki pehle se hi 10 timen vahaan raahat or bachaav ke kaam main lagi hai lekin ise or tej karne ke liye chah or timen bheji ja rahi hai
 Ten helicopters of the Air Force are also flying over Kathmandu and Pokhara for relief and rescue
 
 
 bhartiya team yuddh str par bachaav or raahat kaary main lagi hui he
 The central government is constantly monitoring all the activities
 sarkaar ke saath swanyasevi sanghathan bhi sakriy ho gaye hai
 Many people on Twitter also ran a hashtag of Thank You PM and PM Modi also said that thanks to the tradition of Army and our service
 bharat kii pahal ke baad ab duniya ke tamaam desh or sanyukt raashtra kii agenciyaan bhi nepal kii madad ke liye sakriy ho gai hai
 China has also sent a search team of 62 members
 china ne bhi apatkaaleen tambu, janarator or kambal kapade bheje hai
 China has announced a grant amount of 3 million dollars
 israel ne bhi 260 sadasyon kii team bheji hai jisamen 122 doctor, nurse or paramedics hai
 Apart from this, Pakistan, Britain, Bhutan, Japan, Singapore, Malaysia, many small big countries have come forward to help Nepal
 sanyukt raashtra kii agenciyon ke mutabik haalat itani kharaab he ki kathmandu sahit nepal ke gramin ilaakon main maheenon tak khaane pine or dawa kaa intazaam karnaa hoga
 In India too, 72 people have died due to earthquake
 bihar ke sitamarhi, purvi champaran or darbhanga main zyada nuksaan hua he
 Many people have also been injured in Siliguri in West Bengal
 bharat kii sansad ne nepal ke shok ke saath apni samvednaa jataai he or sabhi dalon ke saansadon ne tay kiya he ki ve apana ek maheene kaa vetan nepal or bharat main punarvaas kaam ke liye denge
 The mps whom we have been criticizing day and night have also come forward
 vekainya naidu ke is prastaav ko sabane ek pal main maan liya
 No one can tell when an earthquake will occur, but everyone knows that there will be an earthquake in the Himalayan region
 vaigyanikon ke mutabik qareeb pachaas karod saal pehle dharti do bade mahadwipon main banty hui thi
 
 
 Eurasia and Gondwana Land
 dharti ke vikaas kram main gondvanaa land kai tukdon main tuutakar alag-alag dishaao kii ore badha
 a part of it which became the Indian subcontinent collided with the Eurasian Plate
 donon platon ke bich isi takkar or ragad se bani silavaton se himalay bana he
 The Indian plate is still under pressure on the Eurasian plate at the rate of five centimeters per year, or rather, sliding under it
 donon platon ke bich bad rahe is dabaav main chuphi urja rah rahakar jab release hoti he to yahaan bukamp aate hai
 There have been earthquakes of around eight magnitude in this Himalayan region
 jaise 1905 main kangra, 1934 main bihar-nepal border, 1897 main shilong or 1950 main assam
 But the red streak that you are seeing in this graphics, there has not been an earthquake of magnitude eight in the last two hundred years
 isi lakeer ke purvi chor par haal main bukamp aayaa he
 According to geologists, this red streak, called the Central Psychological Gap, is prone to a large earthquake because there is a lot of pressure below the ground and its energy can take the shape of an earthquake at any time
 is laal lakeer yani central sizmik gap se hindustan kaa bada hissaa laga hua he
 The Himalayan region is an active zone, but Gondwana is six hundred million years old, which is the most stable and permanent land plot in the world
 maharashtra ke koyna or latur main aaye bukamp ne sabko chaunkaa diya tha
 At present, all of us are stuck in the Himalayan and Eurasia Plate push
 hamaare sapanom kaa makaan lataka hua he
 After every earthquake, we all start feeling homeless in our own home
 jo ghar hamen mahfuz lagata he usee kii chat in dinon jaanaleva lag rahi he
 You have been reading in the newspapers for the last two-three days that large parts of eastern to north India are divided into seismic zones four and five
 jahaan aapkaa ye ankar rahata he or aaj ke ek or penlist rahete hai wo ilaaka to pataa nahin kiske bharose he
 For the last two days, whoever i am looking at, is looking at his flat with suspicion
 export bataate hai ki bukamp aane par ghar ke bheetar deevaaron ke kone par baith jaaya jaae
 The head is bowed and if possible be covered with something
 teble ke neeche baithne kii bhi raay di jaati lekin jab apane teble ko dekha to laga ki mushkil se ye crockeri kii nazaakat sambhaal paata he kancreet se to or dab jayega
 So leaving the corner and the table, your anchor ran towards the elevator, when he realized that the lift was dangerous, he started descending the stairs
 do baar yah galati doharaai
 i was not alone when i came out
 meri hi tarah zyaadaatar logon ne saim harakat kii thi
 The comments agar yah bukamp prabhavit ilaaka he to hamen baar-baar shikshit hone kii zarurat he
 It is not just about tall buildings, whether the street locality and shop buildings are safe or not, whether it is built on the basis of any guideline or not, it is a constant need to know and see
 japan main to duniya kaa bees pratishat bukamp aata he
 The intensity of earthquake here is 6 or more
 har saal kul milakar 2000 se zyada jatke aate rahete hai

 bukamp se kam log mare the

 har maheene skool main dril hoti he
